        <script language="JavaScript1.2" type="text/javascript">
         var Site = "3ders";
    var Path = "pricecompare-3dprinters";
    var nJ = 0;
    function getVer() {
        var v = navigator.appVersion;
        return (v.indexOf("MSIE") &gt; 0) ?
                                v.substring(v.indexOf("MSIE") + 5, v.indexOf("MSIE") + 6) :
                                v.substring(0, v.indexOf(" "));
    }
    function sitetraq(S, P) {
        var ver = getVer();
        var r = "http://stats.sitetraq.nl/sitetraq.count?site=" + escape(S) + "&amp;path=" + escape(P);
        var ref;
        if (top &amp;&amp; top.document &amp;&amp; top.document.referrer)
            ref = top.document.referrer;
        else
            ref = document.referrer;
        r += "&amp;ref=" + escape(ref);
        if (3 &lt; ver &amp;&amp; screen.availWidth &gt; 0) {
            r += ("&amp;size1=" + screen.availWidth + "x" + screen.availHeight);
            r += ("&amp;size2=" + screen.width + "x" + screen.height);
            r += ("&amp;clr=" + screen.colorDepth);
        }
        document.write("&lt;img src='" + r + "' width=1 height=1 border=0&gt;");
    }
    sitetraq(Site, Path);
        </script>
